let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;

const brainToggle = document.getElementById("brainToggle");
const lockSizeBtn = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
const widthInput = document.getElementById("canvasWidth");
const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

const allToolButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".tool-button");
const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
}

function activateBrainMode() {
  brainMode = true;
  brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
  brainToggle.disabled = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";
  console.log("Brain mode activated");
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

// Element injection logic
function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  let el;
  switch(type) {
    case "round-radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      el.style.margin = "10px";
      break;
    case "square-radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      el.style.margin = "10px";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      el.style.margin = "10px";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      el.rows = 3;
      el.cols = 25;
      el.style.margin = "10px";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      el.style.margin = "10px";
      break;
  }
  if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
}

document.getElementById("roundBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("round-radio"));
document.getElementById("squareBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("square-radio"));
document.getElementById("textBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
document.getElementById("multiBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
document.getElementById("dropBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));

brainToggle.addEventListener("click", activateBrainMode);
lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);

// disable everything until unlocked
disableTools(true);

---

âœ… Iâ€™ve reviewed the error and the code â€” here's the full diagnosis:

âŒ ERROR ANALYSIS
ğŸ”¥ Error:
javascript
Copy
Edit
Uncaught TypeError: Cannot read properties of null (reading 'addEventListener')

ğŸ” Location:
js
Copy
Edit
document.getElementById("roundBtn").addEventListener(...)

ğŸ“Œ Meaning:

That button ID (roundBtn) does not exist in your index.html, so when JavaScript tries to attach an event listener to it, it throws an error and breaks the rest of the script, including the Brain Mode logic.

ğŸ’¥ Root Cause:

We added button logic in main.js for these IDs:

js
Copy
Edit
roundBtn
squareBtn
textBtn
multiBtn
dropBtn


But in index.html, the only button that still had a matching ID was the first one. The rest either:

Were removed

Got duplicated improperly

Never had IDs in the first place

So when your script hits those lines, getElementById() returns null, and JS throws a fatal error.

âœ… How to Fix It:

Make sure every button exists with the right id:

html
Copy
Edit
<button id="roundBtn" class="tool-button">Set Round Radio Button</button>
<button id="squareBtn" class="tool-button">Set Square Radio Button</button>
<button id="textBtn" class="tool-button">Set Single Text Line</button>
<button id="multiBtn" class="tool-button">Set Multi Line Text Area</button>
<button id="dropBtn" class="tool-button">Set Drop Down Menu</button>


Put those inside the bottom row where they belong

ğŸ§  Why It Broke the Brain:

Because the error happened early in the script, it prevented brainToggle.addEventListener(...) from ever being executed. So when you clicked â€œTurn Brain ON,â€ nothing happened â€” the listener was never connected.

âœ… Fix Plan:

I'll rebuild v6.4:

All injection buttons restored and properly IDâ€™d

Error-proofed so logic never breaks again

Brain toggle will activate as expected

Ready to push the patch?

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {
  backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};

const brainToggle = document.getElementById("brainToggle");
const lockSizeBtn = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
const exportBtn = document.getElementById("exportBtn");
const resetBtn = document.getElementById("resetBtn");
const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
const widthInput = document.getElementById("canvasWidth");
const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

const allToolButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".tool-button");
const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
  if (exportBtn) exportBtn.disabled = disabled;
}

function saveBrainToLocal() {
  localStorage.setItem("eui_brain", JSON.stringify(brain));
  console.log("ğŸ§  Brain saved to localStorage:", brain);
}

function activateBrainMode() {
  brainMode = true;
  brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
  brainToggle.disabled = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";

  const saved = localStorage.getItem("eui_brain");
  if (saved) {
    try {
      const savedBrain = JSON.parse(saved);
      if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
        widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
        heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
        canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
        canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
        brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
        brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
        canvasLocked = true;
        document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
        disableTools(false);
      }
      if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
        brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
      }
      if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
        brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
        for (const elData of brain.elements) {
          const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
          if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
        }
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.warn("Failed to restore brain from storage:", err);
    }
  }

  console.log("Brain mode activated");
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

document.getElementById("roundBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
document.getElementById("squareBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
document.getElementById("textBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
document.getElementById("multiBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
document.getElementById("dropBtn").addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));

brainToggle.addEventListener("click", activateBrainMode);
lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);
disableTools(true);
})();

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {
  backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};

const brainToggle = document.getElementById("brainToggle");
const lockSizeBtn = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
const exportBtn = document.getElementById("exportBtn");
const resetBtn = document.getElementById("resetBtn");
const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
const widthInput = document.getElementById("canvasWidth");
const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

const allToolButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".tool-button");
const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
  if (exportBtn) exportBtn.disabled = disabled;
}

function saveBrainToLocal() {
  localStorage.setItem("eui_brain", JSON.stringify(brain));
  console.log("ğŸ§  Brain saved to localStorage:", brain);
}

function initializeFromStorage() {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem("eui_brain");
  if (!saved) return;
  try {
    const savedBrain = JSON.parse(saved);
    if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
      widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
      canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
      brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvasLocked = true;
      disableTools(false);
      document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
    }
    if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
      brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
      brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
      for (const elData of brain.elements) {
        const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
        if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
      }
    }
    brainMode = true;
    if (brainToggle) {
      brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
      brainToggle.disabled = true;
    }
    console.log("Brain auto-restored and active.");
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("Failed to auto-restore brain from localStorage:", err);
  }
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

const roundBtn = document.getElementById("roundBtn");
if (roundBtn) roundBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
const squareBtn = document.getElementById("squareBtn");
if (squareBtn) squareBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
const textBtn = document.getElementById("textBtn");
if (textBtn) textBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
const multiBtn = document.getElementById("multiBtn");
if (multiBtn) multiBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
const dropBtn = document.getElementById("dropBtn");
if (dropBtn) dropBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));

if (brainToggle) brainToggle.addEventListener("click", activateBrainMode);
if (lockSizeBtn) lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);

initializeFromStorage();
})();

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {
  backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};

const brainToggle = document.getElementById("brainToggle");
const lockSizeBtn = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
const exportBtn = document.getElementById("exportBtn");
const resetBtn = document.getElementById("resetBtn");
const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
const widthInput = document.getElementById("canvasWidth");
const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

const allToolButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".tool-button");
const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
  if (exportBtn) exportBtn.disabled = disabled;
}

function saveBrainToLocal() {
  localStorage.setItem("eui_brain", JSON.stringify(brain));
  console.log("ğŸ§  Brain saved to localStorage:", brain);
}

function initializeFromStorage() {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem("eui_brain");
  if (!saved) return;
  try {
    const savedBrain = JSON.parse(saved);
    if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
      widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
      canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
      brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvasLocked = true;
      disableTools(false);
      document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
    }
    if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
      brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
      brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
      for (const elData of brain.elements) {
        const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
        if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
      }
    }
    brainMode = true;
    if (brainToggle) {
      brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
      brainToggle.disabled = true;
    }
    console.log("Brain auto-restored and active.");
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("Failed to auto-restore brain from localStorage:", err);
  }
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

const roundBtn = document.getElementById("roundBtn");
if (roundBtn) roundBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
const squareBtn = document.getElementById("squareBtn");
if (squareBtn) squareBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
const textBtn = document.getElementById("textBtn");
if (textBtn) textBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
const multiBtn = document.getElementById("multiBtn");
if (multiBtn) multiBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
const dropBtn = document.getElementById("dropBtn");
if (dropBtn) dropBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));


if (brainToggle) {
  brainToggle.addEventListener("click", () => {
    brainMode = true;
    brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
    brainToggle.disabled = true;
    document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";
    console.log("Brain manually activated.");
  });
}

if (lockSizeBtn) lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);

function activateBrainMode() {
  initializeFromStorage();
}

initializeFromStorage();
})();

const uploadBtn = document.getElementById("uploadBtn");
const uploadInput = document.getElementById("uploadInput");

if (uploadBtn && uploadInput) {
  uploadBtn.addEventListener("click", () => uploadInput.click());
  uploadInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(event) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
        if (!data.canvas || !data.canvas.width || !data.canvas.height) {
          alert("Invalid brain file format.");
          return;
        }
        // clear canvas
        canvas.innerHTML = "";
        brain.canvasWidth = data.canvas.width;
        brain.canvasHeight = data.canvas.height;
        canvas.style.width = data.canvas.width + "px";
        canvas.style.height = data.canvas.height + "px";
        canvasLocked = true;
        brainMode = true;
        brain.backgroundColor = data.canvas.backgroundColor || "#ffffff";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = brain.backgroundColor;
        brain.elements = data.elements || [];
        brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
        brainToggle.disabled = true;
        document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
        disableTools(false);
        // recreate elements
        for (const elData of brain.elements) {
          const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
          if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
        }
        saveBrainToLocal();
        console.log("ğŸ§  Brain file uploaded and restored.");
      } catch (err) {
        alert("Failed to read brain file.");
        console.error(err);
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  });
}

const uploadBtn = document.getElementById("uploadBtn");
const uploadInput = document.getElementById("uploadInput");

if (uploadBtn && uploadInput) {
  uploadBtn.addEventListener("click", () => uploadInput.click());
  uploadInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(event) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
        console.log("ğŸ§  Loaded file content:", data);

        if (!data.canvas || !data.canvas.width || !data.canvas.height) {
          alert("Invalid brain file format.");
          return;
        }

        console.log("ğŸ” Clearing canvas...");
        canvas.innerHTML = "";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = "#ffffff";

        // Set canvas dimensions
        brain.canvasWidth = data.canvas.width;
        brain.canvasHeight = data.canvas.height;
        canvas.style.width = data.canvas.width + "px";
        canvas.style.height = data.canvas.height + "px";
        console.log(ğŸ“ Canvas set to ${data.canvas.width}x${data.canvas.height});

        // Background color
        brain.backgroundColor = data.canvas.backgroundColor || "#ffffff";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = brain.backgroundColor;
        console.log(ğŸ¨ Background color set to ${brain.backgroundColor});

        // Set state flags
        canvasLocked = true;
        brainMode = true;

        // Update button and controls
        if (brainToggle) {
          brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
          brainToggle.disabled = true;
        }
        const controls = document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls");
        if (controls) controls.style.display = "none";

        disableTools(false);

        // Inject elements
        brain.elements = data.elements || [];
        console.log("ğŸ“¦ Restoring elements:", brain.elements);

        for (const elData of brain.elements) {
          const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
          if (el) {
            canvas.appendChild(el);
            console.log(ğŸ§© Injected element: ${elData.type} (ID: ${elData.id}));
          } else {
            console.warn(âš ï¸ Failed to inject element:, elData);
          }
        }

        saveBrainToLocal();
        console.log("âœ… Upload complete. Brain restored and saved.");
      } catch (err) {
        alert("Failed to read brain file.");
        console.error("âŒ Error parsing brain file:", err);
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  });
}

function logToTracker(msg) {
  const logEl = document.getElementById("trackerLog");

    logEl.appendChild(line);
    logEl.scrollTop = logEl.scrollHeight;
  }
}

Youâ€™re absolutely right â€” the issue was crystal clear:

âŒ The same variables (uploadBtn and uploadInput) were declared twice

ğŸ§¨ Root Cause:
js
Copy
Edit

...was declared again at the bottom of the script â€” even though it was already declared earlier.

JavaScript doesn't allow redeclaring a const in the same scope, so it threw:

"Uncaught SyntaxError: Identifier 'uploadBtn' has already been declared"

ğŸ› ï¸ Permanent Fix Strategy:

âœ… NEVER redeclare element bindings like uploadBtn, uploadInput, etc.

âœ… Always declare once at the top and reuse

âœ… Wrap feature modules in IIFEs or dedicated initUploadTracker() style functions if needed

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {
  backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};

const brainToggle = document.getElementById("brainToggle");
const lockSizeBtn = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
const exportBtn = document.getElementById("exportBtn");
const resetBtn = document.getElementById("resetBtn");
const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
const widthInput = document.getElementById("canvasWidth");
const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

const allToolButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".tool-button");
const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
  if (exportBtn) exportBtn.disabled = disabled;
}

function saveBrainToLocal() {
  localStorage.setItem("eui_brain", JSON.stringify(brain));
  console.log("ğŸ§  Brain saved to localStorage:", brain);
}

function initializeFromStorage() {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem("eui_brain");
  if (!saved) return;
  try {
    const savedBrain = JSON.parse(saved);
    if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
      widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
      canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
      brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvasLocked = true;
      disableTools(false);
      document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
    }
    if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
      brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
      brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
      for (const elData of brain.elements) {
        const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
        if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
      }
    }
    brainMode = true;
    if (brainToggle) {
      brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
      brainToggle.disabled = true;
    }
    console.log("Brain auto-restored and active.");
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("Failed to auto-restore brain from localStorage:", err);
  }
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

const roundBtn = document.getElementById("roundBtn");
if (roundBtn) roundBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
const squareBtn = document.getElementById("squareBtn");
if (squareBtn) squareBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
const textBtn = document.getElementById("textBtn");
if (textBtn) textBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
const multiBtn = document.getElementById("multiBtn");
if (multiBtn) multiBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
const dropBtn = document.getElementById("dropBtn");
if (dropBtn) dropBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));


if (brainToggle) {
  brainToggle.addEventListener("click", () => {
    brainMode = true;
    brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
    brainToggle.disabled = true;
    document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";
    console.log("Brain manually activated.");
  });
}

if (lockSizeBtn) lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);

function activateBrainMode() {
  initializeFromStorage();
}

initializeFromStorage();
})();

const uploadBtn = document.getElementById("uploadBtn");
const uploadInput = document.getElementById("uploadInput");

if (uploadBtn && uploadInput) {
  uploadBtn.addEventListener("click", () => uploadInput.click());
  uploadInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(event) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
        if (!data.canvas || !data.canvas.width || !data.canvas.height) {
          alert("Invalid brain file format.");
          return;
        }
        // clear canvas
        canvas.innerHTML = "";
        brain.canvasWidth = data.canvas.width;
        brain.canvasHeight = data.canvas.height;
        canvas.style.width = data.canvas.width + "px";
        canvas.style.height = data.canvas.height + "px";
        canvasLocked = true;
        brainMode = true;
        brain.backgroundColor = data.canvas.backgroundColor || "#ffffff";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = brain.backgroundColor;
        brain.elements = data.elements || [];
        brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
        brainToggle.disabled = true;
        document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
        disableTools(false);
        // recreate elements
        for (const elData of brain.elements) {
          const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
          if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
        }
        saveBrainToLocal();
        console.log("ğŸ§  Brain file uploaded and restored.");
      } catch (err) {
        alert("Failed to read brain file.");
        console.error(err);
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  });
}

function logToTracker(msg) {
  const logEl = document.getElementById("trackerLog");
  if (logEl) {
    const line = document.createElement("div");
    line.textContent = [${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${msg};
    logEl.appendChild(line);
    logEl.scrollTop = logEl.scrollHeight;
  }
}

const uploadBtn = document.getElementById("uploadBtn");
const uploadInput = document.getElementById("uploadInput");

if (uploadBtn && uploadInput) {
  uploadBtn.addEventListener("click", () => uploadInput.click());
  uploadInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    logToTracker("ğŸ“‚ File selected for upload.");
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(event) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
        console.log("ğŸ§  Loaded file content:", data);

        if (!data.canvas || !data.canvas.width || !data.canvas.height) {
          alert("Invalid brain file format.");

        logToTracker("ğŸ” Clearing canvas...");
        canvas.innerHTML = "";

const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
  if (exportBtn) exportBtn.disabled = disabled;
}

function saveBrainToLocal() {
  localStorage.setItem("eui_brain", JSON.stringify(brain));
  console.log("ğŸ§  Brain saved to localStorage:", brain);
}

function initializeFromStorage() {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem("eui_brain");
  if (!saved) return;
  try {
    const savedBrain = JSON.parse(saved);
    if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
      widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
      canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
      brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvasLocked = true;
      disableTools(false);
      document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
    }
    if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
      brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
      brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
      for (const elData of brain.elements) {
        const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
        if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
      }
    }
    brainMode = true;
    if (brainToggle) {
      brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
      brainToggle.disabled = true;
    }
    console.log("Brain auto-restored and active.");
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("Failed to auto-restore brain from localStorage:", err);
  }
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

const roundBtn = document.getElementById("roundBtn");
if (roundBtn) roundBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
const squareBtn = document.getElementById("squareBtn");
if (squareBtn) squareBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
const textBtn = document.getElementById("textBtn");
if (textBtn) textBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
const multiBtn = document.getElementById("multiBtn");
if (multiBtn) multiBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
const dropBtn = document.getElementById("dropBtn");
if (dropBtn) dropBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));


if (brainToggle) {
  brainToggle.addEventListener("click", () => {
    brainMode = true;
    brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
    brainToggle.disabled = true;
    document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";
    console.log("Brain manually activated.");
  });
}

if (lockSizeBtn) lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);

function activateBrainMode() {
  initializeFromStorage();
}

initializeFromStorage();
})();

const uploadBtn = document.getElementById("uploadBtn");
const uploadInput = document.getElementById("uploadInput");

if (uploadBtn && uploadInput) {
  uploadBtn.addEventListener("click", () => uploadInput.click());
  uploadInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(event) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
        if (!data.canvas || !data.canvas.width || !data.canvas.height) {
          alert("Invalid brain file format.");
          return;
        }
        // clear canvas
        canvas.innerHTML = "";
        brain.canvasWidth = data.canvas.width;
        brain.canvasHeight = data.canvas.height;
        canvas.style.width = data.canvas.width + "px";
        canvas.style.height = data.canvas.height + "px";
        canvasLocked = true;
        brainMode = true;
        brain.backgroundColor = data.canvas.backgroundColor || "#ffffff";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = brain.backgroundColor;
        brain.elements = data.elements || [];
        brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
        brainToggle.disabled = true;
        document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
        disableTools(false);
        // recreate elements
        for (const elData of brain.elements) {
          const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
          if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
        }
        saveBrainToLocal();
        console.log("ğŸ§  Brain file uploaded and restored.");
      } catch (err) {
        alert("Failed to read brain file.");
        console.error(err);
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  });
}

function logToTracker(msg) {
  const logEl = document.getElementById("trackerLog");
  if (logEl) {
    const line = document.createElement("div");
    line.textContent = [${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${msg};
    logEl.appendChild(line);
    logEl.scrollTop = logEl.scrollHeight;
  }
}

const uploadBtn = document.getElementById("uploadBtn");
const uploadInput = document.getElementById("uploadInput");

if (uploadBtn && uploadInput) {
  uploadBtn.addEventListener("click", () => uploadInput.click());
  uploadInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    logToTracker("ğŸ“‚ File selected for upload.");
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(event) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
        console.log("ğŸ§  Loaded file content:", data);

        if (!data.canvas || !data.canvas.width || !data.canvas.height) {
          alert("Invalid brain file format.");
          return;
        }

        logToTracker("ğŸ” Clearing canvas...");
        canvas.innerHTML = "";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = "#ffffff";

        brain.canvasWidth = data.canvas.width;
        brain.canvasHeight = data.canvas.height;
        canvas.style.width = data.canvas.width + "px";
        canvas.style.height = data.canvas.height + "px";
        logToTracker(ğŸ“ Canvas set to ${data.canvas.width}x${data.canvas.height});

        brain.backgroundColor = data.canvas.backgroundColor || "#ffffff";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = brain.backgroundColor;
        logToTracker(ğŸ¨ Background color set to ${brain.backgroundColor});

        canvasLocked = true;
        brainMode = true;

        if (brainToggle) {
          brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
          brainToggle.disabled = true;
        }

        const controls = document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls");
        if (controls) controls.style.display = "none";
        disableTools(false);

        brain.elements = data.elements || [];
        logToTracker(ğŸ“¦ Restoring ${brain.elements.length} elements);

        for (const elData of brain.elements) {
          const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
          if (el) {
            canvas.appendChild(el);
            logToTracker(ğŸ§© Injected element: ${elData.type} (ID: ${elData.id}));
          } else {
            console.warn("âš ï¸ Failed to inject:", elData);
          }
        }

        saveBrainToLocal();
        logToTracker("âœ… Upload complete. Brain restored.");
      } catch (err) {
        alert("Failed to read brain file.");
        console.error("âŒ Error parsing brain file:", err);
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  });
}

// Inject event tracking
document.querySelectorAll("button.tool-button").forEach(btn => {
  btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    logToTracker(ğŸŸ¢ Clicked: ${btn.textContent.trim()});
  });
});

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    logToTracker("ğŸ§¹ Reset template triggered.");
  });
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      logToTracker(ğŸ¨ Color changed to ${swatch.style.backgroundColor});
    }
  });
});

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {
  backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};

function logToTracker(msg) {
  const logEl = document.getElementById("trackerLog");

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {
  backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};

const brainToggle = document.getElementById("brainToggle");
const lockSizeBtn = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
const exportBtn = document.getElementById("exportBtn");
const resetBtn = document.getElementById("resetBtn");
const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
const widthInput = document.getElementById("canvasWidth");
const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

const allToolButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".tool-button");
const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
  if (exportBtn) exportBtn.disabled = disabled;
}

function saveBrainToLocal() {
  localStorage.setItem("eui_brain", JSON.stringify(brain));
  console.log("ğŸ§  Brain saved to localStorage:", brain);
}

function initializeFromStorage() {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem("eui_brain");
  if (!saved) return;
  try {
    const savedBrain = JSON.parse(saved);
    if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
      widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
      canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
      brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvasLocked = true;
      disableTools(false);
      document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
    }
    if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
      brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
      brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
      for (const elData of brain.elements) {
        const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
        if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
      }
    }
    brainMode = true;
    if (brainToggle) {
      brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
      brainToggle.disabled = true;
    }
    console.log("Brain auto-restored and active.");
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("Failed to auto-restore brain from localStorage:", err);
  }
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

const roundBtn = document.getElementById("roundBtn");
if (roundBtn) roundBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
const squareBtn = document.getElementById("squareBtn");
if (squareBtn) squareBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
const textBtn = document.getElementById("textBtn");
if (textBtn) textBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
const multiBtn = document.getElementById("multiBtn");
if (multiBtn) multiBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
const dropBtn = document.getElementById("dropBtn");
if (dropBtn) dropBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));


if (brainToggle) {
  brainToggle.addEventListener("click", () => {
    brainMode = true;
    brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
    brainToggle.disabled = true;
    document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";
    console.log("Brain manually activated.");
  });
}

if (lockSizeBtn) lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);

function activateBrainMode() {
  initializeFromStorage();
}

initializeFromStorage();
})();

const uploadBtn = document.getElementById("uploadBtn");
const uploadInput = document.getElementById("uploadInput");

if (uploadBtn && uploadInput) {
  uploadBtn.addEventListener("click", () => uploadInput.click());
  uploadInput.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(event) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
        if (!data.canvas || !data.canvas.width || !data.canvas.height) {
          alert("Invalid brain file format.");
          return;
        }
        // clear canvas
        canvas.innerHTML = "";
        brain.canvasWidth = data.canvas.width;
        brain.canvasHeight = data.canvas.height;
        canvas.style.width = data.canvas.width + "px";
        canvas.style.height = data.canvas.height + "px";
        canvasLocked = true;
        brainMode = true;
        brain.backgroundColor = data.canvas.backgroundColor || "#ffffff";
        canvas.style.backgroundColor = brain.backgroundColor;
        brain.elements = data.elements || [];
        brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
        brainToggle.disabled = true;
        document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
        disableTools(false);
        // recreate elements
        for (const elData of brain.elements) {
          const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
          if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
        }
        saveBrainToLocal();
        console.log("ğŸ§  Brain file uploaded and restored.");
      } catch (err) {
        alert("Failed to read brain file.");
        console.error(err);
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  });
}

function logToTracker(msg) {
  const logEl = document.getElementById("trackerLog");
  if (logEl) {
    const line = document.createElement("div");
    line.textContent = [${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${msg};
    logEl.appendChild(line);
    logEl.scrollTop = logEl.scrollHeight;
  }
}

// Declare once, no repeats

// Load brain from local storage
function loadBrainFromLocal() {
  chrome.storage.local.get("brain_live", (data) => {
    if (data.brain_live) {
      try {
        const savedBrain = JSON.parse(data.brain_live);
        if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
          widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
          heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
          canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
          canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
          brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
          brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
          canvasLocked = true;
          document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
          disableTools(false);
        }
        if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
          canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
          brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
        }
        if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
          brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
          for (const elData of brain.elements) {
            const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
            if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
          }
        }
        brainMode = true;
        if (brainToggle) {
          brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
          brainToggle.disabled = true;
        }
        console.log("ğŸ§  Brain restored from internal memory.");
      } catch (err) {
        console.warn("âš ï¸ Failed to parse local brain data:", err);
      }
    }
  });
}

// On extension load, try to restore from local first
loadBrainFromLocal();
          backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};

const brainToggle = document.getElementById("brainToggle");
const lockSizeBtn = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
const exportBtn = document.getElementById("exportBtn");
const resetBtn = document.getElementById("resetBtn");
const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
const widthInput = document.getElementById("canvasWidth");
const heightInput = document.getElementById("canvasHeight");

const allToolButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".tool-button");
const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");

function disableTools(disabled) {
  allToolButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = disabled);
  swatches.forEach(s => s.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? "none" : "auto");
  if (exportBtn) exportBtn.disabled = disabled;
}

function saveBrainToLocal() {
  localStorage.setItem("eui_brain", JSON.stringify(brain));
  console.log("ğŸ§  Brain saved to localStorage:", brain);
}

function initializeFromStorage() {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem("eui_brain");
  if (!saved) return;
  try {
    const savedBrain = JSON.parse(saved);
    if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
      widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
      canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
      brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
      brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
      canvasLocked = true;
      disableTools(false);
      document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
    }
    if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
      brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
      brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
      for (const elData of brain.elements) {
        const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
        if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
      }
    }
    brainMode = true;
    if (brainToggle) {
      brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
      brainToggle.disabled = true;
    }
    console.log("Brain auto-restored and active.");
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("Failed to auto-restore brain from localStorage:", err);
  }
}

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

const roundBtn = document.getElementById("roundBtn");
if (roundBtn) roundBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
const squareBtn = document.getElementById("squareBtn");
if (squareBtn) squareBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
const textBtn = document.getElementById("textBtn");
if (textBtn) textBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
const multiBtn = document.getElementById("multiBtn");
if (multiBtn) multiBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
const dropBtn = document.getElementById("dropBtn");
if (dropBtn) dropBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));


if (brainToggle) {
  brainToggle.addEventListener("click", () => {
    brainMode = true;
    brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
    brainToggle.disabled = true;
    document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";
    console.log("Brain manually activated.");
  });
}

if (lockSizeBtn) lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);

function activateBrainMode() {
  initializeFromStorage();
}

initializeFromStorage();
})();



// Auto-start tracker when extension loads
(function initTracker() {
  function logToTracker(msg) {
    const logEl = document.getElementById("trackerLog");
    if (!logEl) return;
    const line = document.createElement("div");
    line.textContent = [${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${msg};
    logEl.appendChild(line);
    logEl.scrollTop = logEl.scrollHeight;
  }

  const buttons = document.querySelectorAll("button.tool-button");
  buttons.forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      logToTracker(ğŸŸ¢ Clicked: ${btn.textContent.trim()});
    });
  });

  const swatches = document.querySelectorAll(".swatch");
  swatches.forEach(swatch => {
    swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
      logToTracker(ğŸ¨ Swatch: ${swatch.style.backgroundColor});
    });
  });

  const reset = document.getElementById("resetBtn");
  if (reset) {
    reset.addEventListener("click", () => {
      logToTracker("ğŸ§¹ Reset triggered");
    });
  }

  const lock = document.getElementById("lockCanvasSize");
  if (lock) {
    lock.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const w = document.getElementById("canvasWidth")?.value || "?";
      const h = document.getElementById("canvasHeight")?.value || "?";
      logToTracker(ğŸ“ Canvas locked at ${w}x${h});
    });
  }

  logToTracker("ğŸ§  Tracker activated");
})();

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {

// Auto-save brain to Chrome local storage
    console.log("ğŸ§  Auto-saved brain to local storage.");
  });
}

// Load brain from local storage
function loadBrainFromLocal() {
  chrome.storage.local.get("brain_live", (data) => {
    if (data.brain_live) {
      try {
        const savedBrain = JSON.parse(data.brain_live);
        if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
          widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
          heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
          canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
          canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
          brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
          brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
          canvasLocked = true;
          document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
          disableTools(false);
        }
        if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
          canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
          brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
        }
        if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
          brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
          for (const elData of brain.elements) {
            const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
            if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
          }
        }
        brainMode = true;
        if (brainToggle) {
          brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
          brainToggle.disabled = true;
        }
        console.log("ğŸ§  Brain restored from internal memory.");
      } catch (err) {
        console.warn("âš ï¸ Failed to parse local brain data:", err);
      }
    }
  });
}

// On extension load, try to restore from local first
loadBrainFromLocal();
          backgroundColor: null,

function lockCanvasSize() {
  const width = parseInt(widthInput.value);
  const height = parseInt(heightInput.value);
  if (isNaN(width) || isNaN(height) || width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
    alert("Invalid canvas size");
    return;
  }
  canvas.style.width = width + "px";
  canvas.style.height = height + "px";
  brain.canvasWidth = width;
  brain.canvasHeight = height;
  canvasLocked = true;
  document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
  disableTools(false);
  saveBrainToLocal();
  console.log(Canvas locked at ${width}x${height});
}

swatches.forEach(swatch => {
  swatch.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (brainMode && canvasLocked) {
      const color = swatch.style.backgroundColor;
      canvas.style.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      brain.backgroundColor = color;
      saveBrainToLocal();
      console.log(Canvas background set to ${color});
    }
  });
});

function exportBrainFile() {
  if (!brain.backgroundColor) {
    alert("No canvas data to export yet.");
    return;
  }
  const data = {
    canvas: {
      width: brain.canvasWidth,
      height: brain.canvasHeight,
      backgroundColor: brain.backgroundColor
    },
    elements: brain.elements,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = url;
  a.download = "eui_brain_file.json";
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

if (resetBtn) {
  resetBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    if (confirm("This will erase your current template. Continue?")) {
      localStorage.removeItem("eui_brain");
      location.reload();
    }
  });
}

function createElementFromType(type, id) {
  let el;
  switch (type) {
    case "radio":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "radio";
      break;
    case "checkbox":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "checkbox";
      break;
    case "text-line":
      el = document.createElement("input");
      el.type = "text";
      el.placeholder = "Single line";
      break;
    case "text-area":
      el = document.createElement("textarea");
      el.placeholder = "Multi-line";
      break;
    case "dropdown":
      el = document.createElement("select");
      ["Option 1", "Option 2", "Option 3"].forEach(txt => {
        const opt = document.createElement("option");
        opt.textContent = txt;
        el.appendChild(opt);
      });
      break;
  }
  if (el) {
    el.id = id;
    el.style.margin = "10px";
  }
  return el;
}

function injectElement(type) {
  if (!(brainMode && canvasLocked)) return;
  const id = "el_" + elementCounter++;
  const el = createElementFromType(type, id);
  if (el) {
    canvas.appendChild(el);
    brain.elements.push({ type, id });
    saveBrainToLocal();
    saveBrainToLocal();
  }
}

const roundBtn = document.getElementById("roundBtn");
if (roundBtn) roundBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("radio"));
const squareBtn = document.getElementById("squareBtn");
if (squareBtn) squareBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("checkbox"));
const textBtn = document.getElementById("textBtn");
if (textBtn) textBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-line"));
const multiBtn = document.getElementById("multiBtn");
if (multiBtn) multiBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("text-area"));
const dropBtn = document.getElementById("dropBtn");
if (dropBtn) dropBtn.addEventListener("click", () => injectElement("dropdown"));


if (brainToggle) {
  brainToggle.addEventListener("click", () => {
    brainMode = true;
    brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
    brainToggle.disabled = true;
    document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "flex";
    console.log("Brain manually activated.");
  });
}

if (lockSizeBtn) lockSizeBtn.addEventListener("click", lockCanvasSize);
if (exportBtn) exportBtn.addEventListener("click", exportBrainFile);

(function() {
let brainMode = false;
let canvasLocked = false;
let elementCounter = 1;

const brain = {

// Auto-save brain to Chrome local storage
    console.log("ğŸ§  Auto-saved brain to local storage.");
  });
}

// Load brain from local storage
function loadBrainFromLocal() {
  chrome.storage.local.get("brain_live", (data) => {
    if (data.brain_live) {
      try {
        const savedBrain = JSON.parse(data.brain_live);
        if (savedBrain.canvasWidth && savedBrain.canvasHeight) {
          widthInput.value = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
          heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
          canvas.style.width = savedBrain.canvasWidth + "px";
          canvas.style.height = savedBrain.canvasHeight + "px";
          brain.canvasWidth = savedBrain.canvasWidth;
          brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;
          canvasLocked = true;
          document.getElementById("canvasSizeControls").style.display = "none";
          disableTools(false);
        }
        if (savedBrain.backgroundColor) {
          canvas.style.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
          brain.backgroundColor = savedBrain.backgroundColor;
        }
        if (Array.isArray(savedBrain.elements)) {
          brain.elements = savedBrain.elements;
          for (const elData of brain.elements) {
            const el = createElementFromType(elData.type, elData.id);
            if (el) canvas.appendChild(el);
          }
        }
        brainMode = true;
        if (brainToggle) {
          brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";
          brainToggle.disabled = true;
        }
        console.log("ğŸ§  Brain restored from internal memory.");
      } catch (err) {
        console.warn("âš ï¸ Failed to parse local brain data:", err);
      }
    }
  });
}

// On extension load, try to restore from local first
loadBrainFromLocal();
          backgroundColor: null,
  canvasWidth: null,
  canvasHeight: null,
  elements: []
};


// âœ… Save to localStorage
function saveBrainToLocal() {
  chrome.storage.local.set({ brain_live: JSON.stringify(brain) }, () => {
    console.log("ğŸ§  Auto-saved brain to local storage.");
  });
}

// âœ… Load from localStorage on extension load
function loadBrainFromLocal() {
  chrome.storage.local.get("brain_live", (data) => {
    if (data.brain_live) {
      try {
        const savedBrain = JSON.parse(data.brain_live);

          heightInput.value = savedBrain.canvasHeight;

          brain.canvasHeight = savedBrain.canvasHeight;

          brainToggle.textContent = "Brain Mode: ON";

      } catch (err) {
        console.warn("âš ï¸ Failed to parse local brain data:", err);

    }
  });
